<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_04f7cab6-be83-401d-ac12-41affe3801d5'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<a href="/questions/480789"><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[?<br />ي مشهد قتل العميد عمر .. صرخ في النهاية مش معقوووووووول لما شاف وجه ادم .. وفي فلاش باك متاخر استنتج الجميع ان حسن هو الجزار .. بعد النهاية الرمادية اللي عملها ادم في مقتل حسن . <br />ثم عاد ادم وفسر لظابط المخابرات سامح انه خدعهم لكي يظنو ان حسن الجزار بعد ما تلاعب بعقله <br />وفسر كل شئ ... الا مقتل العميد عمر لماذا صرخ باستغراب لحظة قتله .. ان كان ادم هو القاتل والعميد كان ينتظر ذلك بهدوء <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></a>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/29265125-rosa-baerle"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1442481449i/29265125._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">دا نفس السؤال اللى بسأله و مش فاهمة ليه بردو !<br/>الفلاش باك جاب لطفى وهو بيقول مش معقول ودا يمكن لإنه اتفاجأ بوجود آدم حي .. لكن عمر هو اللى صرخ رغم فعلا<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">دا نفس السؤال اللى بسأله و مش فاهمة ليه بردو !<br />الفلاش باك جاب لطفى وهو بيقول مش معقول ودا يمكن لإنه اتفاجأ بوجود آدم حي .. لكن عمر هو اللى صرخ رغم فعلا انتظاره لآدم الجزار .. لو لمجرد الحبكة الدرامية عشان يصورلنا ان حسن هو القاتل فى اللحظة دى فلازم يكون فيه مبرر ! و الا هتبقى بايخة منه بصراحة !<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_767335121" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/767335121" />
    <a title="Rania" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2949332-rania"><img alt="Rania" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367335023p2/2949332.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/767335121?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rania" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rania" href="/user/show/2949332-rania">Rania</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer767335121" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5565208036838073979">This book is a crime thriller based for the great part on the Nihilistic quotation with which Ahmed Mourad starts his "Diamond Dust", "The darkest of nations' times is when people think that evil is the only path to reach good". Man invented governments and security bodies so that the world wouldn't turn into a jungle when people avenge themselves on their tormentors, but when the security bodies stop fulfilling their role and the people working for them become the real tormentors, some people f</span>
  <span id="freeText5565208036838073979" style="display:none">This book is a crime thriller based for the great part on the Nihilistic quotation with which Ahmed Mourad starts his "Diamond Dust", "The darkest of nations' times is when people think that evil is the only path to reach good". Man invented governments and security bodies so that the world wouldn't turn into a jungle when people avenge themselves on their tormentors, but when the security bodies stop fulfilling their role and the people working for them become the real tormentors, some people find themselves obliged to take revenge with their very hands, and Adam, the central character in the book, is a case in point. The book is a crime thriller which is full of suspense, but it is also full of flaws. The worst thing about the book is that I got to know before reading it that it is for the most part plagiarized, the author having based his story on the events of some American movies. Worse still, he sort of narrates certain scenes with the very words used in those movies. The writer also has serious problems with both his language and his structuring of the plot. The conversations between characters sound unnatural to a great extent, and a case in point is the "romantic" conversation between the killer and one of his victims. Also, the finding a dead man's corpse in order to be sure he has died is ABC detective stories, and the disappearance of it should arouse the reader's doubts and make him/her suspect who is behind the crimes. In other words, the book is not intelligently written. Still, the writer has a good potential that he may use in other works "of his own creation". </span>
  <a data-text-id="5565208036838073979" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2792136309" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer2736058799567024405">It was a heartbreaking, sad, and enjoyable novel.<br/>I literally had so much fun reading it, because I adore this kind of novels, those are about blood and crimes.<br/> I had finished it in only two days.<br/>This novel was the first I read of Hasan's.<br/>I also bought 'Smile You Are Died', but didn't start reading it yet. <br/><br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2065779118" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2065779118" />
    <a title="lia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54558352-lia"><img alt="lia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460002356p2/54558352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2065779118?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="lia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="lia" href="/user/show/54558352-lia">lia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2065779118" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18165445832386995290">so the book gave me mixed emotions.<br/><br/>interesting. then omg no. then i hope y'all die. then no. then omg woah. then it got boring. like really boring. <br/><br/>i found the middle part not quite fun. <br/>i personally hoped for more gore but yeah. i liked the gore shown though. somehow, i wish there was more to the killer. like more details. more into his mind. i don't know. i didn't feel like i got enough of him or the other characters in general. also, i felt lost at some point because the names were slightly g</span>
  <span id="freeText18165445832386995290" style="display:none">so the book gave me mixed emotions.<br /><br />interesting. then omg no. then i hope y'all die. then no. then omg woah. then it got boring. like really boring. <br /><br />i found the middle part not quite fun. <br />i personally hoped for more gore but yeah. i liked the gore shown though. somehow, i wish there was more to the killer. like more details. more into his mind. i don't know. i didn't feel like i got enough of him or the other characters in general. also, i felt lost at some point because the names were slightly generic.<br /><br />but let's get to what really had me going insane and not in a good way. the ending. i did not at all like the ending. like there was one part that had me woah. this is interesting. i like this. and then the actual thing a few pages later had me flipping tables.<br /><br />also, the writing style wasn't that gripping and i didn't like it much. it didn't flow that smoothly. the way the flashbacks were portrayed, i feel like it could've been smoother. <br />also, one dialogue line had me laughing because i don't think anyone in real life would actually do that. <br /><br />also, it made me ponder a lot on the reality of the society the book takes place in and it just made me angrier (but that's not the reason the book dissapointed me. the ending and the writing style are.) <br /><br />so yeah.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18165445832386995290" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('s9dlTtMi+6evR4P0DRngyLWpfeaFAwyv721Xn3dWr95CKFRbgUbULk1gY7ZE9vKzUhp/4TstsIga2mG44ZOvOw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UwNUjULxkQALoxsdbJiQLqqD4LOJ3Mffi+ACy/1IR02i/GWYEJW+iemE+18ld4JVTTDitDfye/h+VzTsa41HqA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15587465447555826597">أصبح اسمه يتردد على استحياء في أوساط المؤلفين الشباب.. غيرت رواياته مفاهيم كثيرة لعقول الشباب.. اقترن اسمه بعالم الجن والعفاريت والمخطوطات القديمة والقتلة النفسيين وعالم الرعب.. إنه حسن الجندي المؤلف الشاب<br/><br/>على شبكة الإنترنت تخطت نسبة مشاهدات قصصه حاجز المائة ألف قارئ (100 ألف)، حصل على شهرة ليست بالقليلة داخل مصر وخارجها من خلال ثلاثيته (مخطوطة بن إسحاق) والتي وضعت منذ مدة طويلة على المنتديات العرب</span>
  <span id="freeText15587465447555826597" style="display:none">أصبح اسمه يتردد على استحياء في أوساط المؤلفين الشباب.. غيرت رواياته مفاهيم كثيرة لعقول الشباب.. اقترن اسمه بعالم الجن والعفاريت والمخطوطات القديمة والقتلة النفسيين وعالم الرعب.. إنه حسن الجندي المؤلف الشاب<br /><br />على شبكة الإنترنت تخطت نسبة مشاهدات قصصه حاجز المائة ألف قارئ (100 ألف)، حصل على شهرة ليست بالقليلة داخل مصر وخارجها من خلال ثلاثيته (مخطوطة بن إسحاق) والتي وضعت منذ مدة طويلة على المنتديات العربية وانتهت بطباعتها ونزولها المكتبات المصرية، عشقه الألاف من خلال طريقته في الكتابة والتي كان يعمل على تطويرها خلال السنوات السابقة، يتميز بسهولة تعبيراته واهتمامه بعامل التشويق داخل الروايات واختراقه أماكن كثيرة محرمة، يقول في أحد اللقاءات الصحفية أنه تلقى الكثير من الاتصالات والرسائل تطلب منه أرقام هواتف شخصيات معينة في روايته وعندما كان يخبرهم بأنها شخصيات ليست حقيقية كان البعض يصر على أنه يخفي حقيقتها لدواعي أمنية... دائماً ما يقول أنه يحاول أن يوجد نوعاً جديداً من أدب الرعب يناسب العقلية المصرية والعربية ويمكنه أن يفرض نفسه على الساحة العالمية وليس مجرد تقليد أو مسخ للقصص الأوربية عن الرعب والتي تتكلم عن مصاصي الدماء والمتحولين والمذؤوب، يجمع الكثير على أنه استطاع بعد ظهور أولى رواياته أن يثبت أنه يسير على الطريق الصحيح، وبعد صدور الرواية الثانية يعتقد البعض أنها ستكون علامة مميزة في حياة هذا المؤلف</span>
  <a data-text-id="15587465447555826597" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
